        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer135893887" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1465267238167914865"><b>This was Dark!</b> Much darker than most of the other books in this series and it hardly had any funny moments. Also, it takes place at the same time as <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7098304.Demon_from_the_Dark__Immortals_After_Dark___10_' title='Demon from the Dark (Immortals After Dark, #10) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>Demon from the Dark</a>, so I can see where the timeline could be confusing if I had not just recently read it. <b>But I still really liked it, even with all the darkness and the angst.</b><br/><br/>I really loved Declan! Yeah, he did seem evil but the guy <i>really</i> didn't know any better. He had such a tortured, scarred life. I even liked Regin; I never liked her in any o</span>
  <span id="freeText1465267238167914865" style="display:none"><b>This was Dark!</b> Much darker than most of the other books in this series and it hardly had any funny moments. Also, it takes place at the same time as <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7098304.Demon_from_the_Dark__Immortals_After_Dark___10_" title="Demon from the Dark (Immortals After Dark, #10) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Demon from the Dark</a>, so I can see where the timeline could be confusing if I had not just recently read it. <b>But I still really liked it, even with all the darkness and the angst.</b><br /><br />I really loved Declan! Yeah, he did seem evil but the guy <i>really</i> didn't know any better. He had such a tortured, scarred life. I even liked Regin; I never liked her in any of the previous books. They made great enemies-to-lovers and I loved all the sexual tension!<br /><br />My only issue with the book was all the flashbacks and dreams. I guess because of the way the author set up Declan and Regin's relationship the flashbacks were kinda required, but I found them mostly boring. Between the dreams and the flashbacks it seemed to be telling the same story over and over and over!<br /><br />I loved the ending! Once I got to 70% the plot stopped being so predictable (remember, I already know a lot of what happens from reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7098304.Demon_from_the_Dark__Immortals_After_Dark___10_" title="Demon from the Dark (Immortals After Dark, #10) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Demon from the Dark</a>). There were even a few surprises and a bit of a twist in then end. <br /><br />I can't wait for the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10790516-lothaire" rel="nofollow noopener">Enemy of Old</a> to finally get his story next!<br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="1465267238167914865" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText9468592827445718864" style="display:none">What do you do when you love an author so much that you want to give them the acclaim they deserve???<br /><br />You sit around typing, retyping, typing and retyping for long stretches of time trying to put into words why she is so fabulous...and then at the end of all that, you delete everything in complete frustration knowing that it is completely impossible to express how high you feel when reading her work.<br /><br />So in a completely understated manner I will say that "I absolutely love, adore, cherish and worship everything that is Kresley Cole"<br />This book is just another installment in the phenomenal Immortals After Dark series and as with all the others I LOVED IT TO BITS!!! <br /><br />A few of the MANY, MANY, MANY freakishly hilarious favourite quotes from this terrific book:<br /><br />1.     <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/103206862?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♡Karlyn P♡" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p">♡Karlyn P♡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781849830386" href="/book/show/8158993-dreams-of-a-dark-warrior">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=published-2011">published-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=genre-paranromal">genre-paranromal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=read-2011">read-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=steam-hot">steam-hot</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer103206862" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3794933529626994977">The time-line for Dreams of a Dark Warrior parallels with Demon from the Dark, and takes us back to that remote island prison in the Pacific. (In truth, these stories are going on at the same time - so be sure to have read Demon from the Dark first.) Valkyrie Regin the Radiant is being held prisoner by warden Declan Chase, a deeply troubled sexy mortal who believes all immortal creatures are evil and should be destroyed. He is a top member of The Order, an organization led by Webb who will stop </span>
  <span id="freeText3794933529626994977" style="display:none">The time-line for Dreams of a Dark Warrior parallels with Demon from the Dark, and takes us back to that remote island prison in the Pacific. (In truth, these stories are going on at the same time - so be sure to have read Demon from the Dark first.) Valkyrie Regin the Radiant is being held prisoner by warden Declan Chase, a deeply troubled sexy mortal who believes all immortal creatures are evil and should be destroyed. He is a top member of The Order, an organization led by Webb who will stop at nothing to capture and learn about the immortals through vivisection (think of it as an autopsy on the living) and other torturous means.<br /><br />However, Declan Chase is actually Regin's reincarnated lover Aiden, a mortal Viking berserker killed one thousand years ago before they could marry. Over the years, Aiden kept coming back in different forms via reincarnation - only to die again once Regin had found him and restored Aiden's memories with a kiss. So when Regin recognized Chase as her former lover Aiden, she is mortified by his torturous ways and intends to use the kiss of doom against him to help win her freedom. <br /><br />Declan doesn't understand why he is so drawn to Regin, a filthy immortal! But he also doesn't realize he is actually Aiden. Throughout the book Regin and Declan fight their attraction and disgust with each other, which at times made for some great laughs and some good steam! So when chaos rains, Regin, Declan and a clan of immortals fight it out for freedom and revenge.<br /><br />This book was a lot of fun to read. As we have come to expect from this series, it is filled with great action, hot sex scenes, and a mix of regular and new characters. We meet new comers Natalya, a fey, a half-ling high school kid name Thad, and Aiden's best friend Brandr, who won his immortality from the Gods a millennium ago. Nix returns, and as always was on her game! Love her! And we get to know more about vampire Lothaire, who just cracked me up every time he spoke. I am so happy his book is next!!<br /><br />However, there were few aspects that I had issue with which is why I only gave it a B grade. For instance, Declan was a great hero but it took a long time to warm up to him since he was so dark and tortured through much of the book. But when he finally came around and recognized Regin as his woman, I forgave all his crimes against Regin and fell for the guy. However, I also felt many of his crimes against the lore were simply irredeemable. <br /><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The ending was a bit too pat for me, with too much redemption for Chase. Chase made a lot of enemies from the Lore, and many of his actions were unforgivable in my eyes. It will be interesting to see how the Lore interacts with him in future books. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br />Overall, this book was tough to put down! It is a bit darker than previous, including some gruesome torture scenes and possibly the coldest and meanest hero in the series yet. I loved how we got to meet Aiden in several of his reincarnated forms, and Regin was so witty and funny with her cutting dialogue she helped lighten the story and balance it out for a great read. (I think Regin is now my favorite heroine in this series.) And while I didn't warm up to Declan Chase as the book's hero until near the end, I think Regin and him ended up as a great couple. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3794933529626994977" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1103486335" />
    <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads"><img alt="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396922701p2/4561998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1103486335?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads">Carmel (Rabid Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781442369764" href="/book/show/18468048-dreams-of-a-dark-warrior">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio-2015">audio-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103486335" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11891307529257758311"><b>Reviewed by: <a href='http://rabidreads.ca/2015/11/audiobook-review-dreams-of-a-dark-warrior-by-kresley-cole-kresleycole-petkoff-simonaudio.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br/><br/>Immortals have been disappearing for several installments now, and in DREAMS OF A DARK WARRIOR we find out why, so it was nice to get closure to one of this series’ long running secondary threads. Regin has also been one of my favourite IMMORTALS AFTER DARK characters since I first made her acquaintance which made this book extra rewarding for me. Then, enter Lothaire the enigmatic (and sexy!) Enemy of Old, plus the interconnecting of several previous plots, and you have</span>
  <span id="freeText11891307529257758311" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2015/11/audiobook-review-dreams-of-a-dark-warrior-by-kresley-cole-kresleycole-petkoff-simonaudio.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br /><br />Immortals have been disappearing for several installments now, and in DREAMS OF A DARK WARRIOR we find out why, so it was nice to get closure to one of this series’ long running secondary threads. Regin has also been one of my favourite IMMORTALS AFTER DARK characters since I first made her acquaintance which made this book extra rewarding for me. Then, enter Lothaire the enigmatic (and sexy!) Enemy of Old, plus the interconnecting of several previous plots, and you have one happy listener!<br /><br />I absolutely loved the premise; a Berserker warrior falls short of winning his 200th battle, and with it his chance at immortality, as a consequence he’s stuck in an endless reincarnation loop that triggers whenever his memories come flooding back upon reuniting with his soul mate. It’s tragic. It’s sappy. And, I just gobbled it up! Every rebirth brings one of Aidan’s original personality traits to the fore, and Declan Chase represents the worst of him. If you have a thing for damaged heroes, DREAMS OF A DARK WARRIOR is your stop.<br /><br />Regin the Radiant has always been one of this series’ more vocal characters, and I thoroughly enjoyed watching her take center stage as this novel’s female protagonist. She has quite a mouth on her, so I was psyched that Kresley Cole didn’t hold back when it came to her dialogue. Her POV was a riot, but at the same time there was a touch of vulnerability to her as well that helped to ensure that there were as many feels as there were laughs which is equally imperative in Paranormal Romance.<br /><br />Robert Petkoff’s narration was as impressive this tenth time around as it was the first. Chase has an Irish background, so he added yet another accent to his overflowing repertoire, and Lothaire’s Russian cadence was to die for. I’ve only had a tiny taste of what this particular vamp has to offer, but after sampling Petkoff’s rendition I want more! He also excelled at conveying Regin’s energy, and crazy antics, and his surfer dude reading of Thad was pretty gnarly too.<br /><br />I want to marry DREAMS OF A DARK WARRIOR, and have audiobook babies.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_136095537" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/136095537" />
    <a title="Katie(babs)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs"><img alt="Katie(babs)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1242522005p2/179852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/136095537?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie(babs)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie(babs)" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs">Katie(babs)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer136095537&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer136095537" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15052260992574159364">Let me get it out of the way and say that Dreams of a Dark Warrior (book #11) was amazing. Although I did enjoy Demon from the Dark a smidgen more, this is another fabulous addition to Kresley Cole’s very addicting Immortals After Dark series. Many of her fans have been waiting for the match up between Regin the Radiant, the glowing, loud-mouth, “rocks out with her cock out” Valkyrie, and her soul mate, Aidan the Fierce, the berserker who’s reincarnated time and again to find Regin, but it never</span>
  <span id="freeText15052260992574159364" style="display:none">Let me get it out of the way and say that Dreams of a Dark Warrior (book #11) was amazing. Although I did enjoy Demon from the Dark a smidgen more, this is another fabulous addition to Kresley Cole’s very addicting Immortals After Dark series. Many of her fans have been waiting for the match up between Regin the Radiant, the glowing, loud-mouth, “rocks out with her cock out” Valkyrie, and her soul mate, Aidan the Fierce, the berserker who’s reincarnated time and again to find Regin, but it never ends happily for them. Aidan always ends up dead, and Regin spends another few hundred years waiting for the next reincarnation of Aidan to start the whole cycle again. Regin feels both she and Aidan are cursed, never to be together and to suffer alone.<br /><br />Dreams of a Dark Warrior starts with how Regin and Aidan first met. Regin was only twelve at the time, searching for her beloved, missing sister Lucia. Aidan quickly realizes that Regin is his mate and will wait for her to grow up so he can claim her. But these two lovers can’t consummate their relationship. Since Regin is an immortal and Aidan isn’t, he must try to earn his immortality called Ohalla by winning two hundred battles in Woden’s name. Woden is a god and Regin is one of his daughters. Unfortunately Aidan jumps the gun because he can’t control his passion for Regin and the curse between these two unfortunate lovers is engaged.<br /><br />Now in present day, Regin is waiting for the next Aidan reincarnation. But this time she’ll deny him to keep him alive and stop from doing two things with him that always leads to his death once they’re acted upon. But Regin has much more to worry about, because a mortal by the name Declan Chase, who’s part of a secret Order against the creatures of the Lore, will capture Regin and her kind, doing unholy experiments and tortures on them, hoping to eradicate their existence. Declan is filled with hate and wants revenge because of how his family was killed by a group of evil immortals who tortured and left Declan for dead when he was only seventeen. He’s very much a loner who wears black, won’t let anyone see him naked and is addicted to drugs to numb his pain and urges he can’t control for something or someone. And when he comes in contact with Regin, his reasoning flies out the window.<br /><br />Regin figures out who Declan is inside, and in order to save herself and those of the Lore he has captured, she must make him remember his past lives because if she doesn’t, all the immortals could be destroyed for the Accession has arrived in full force.<br /><br />Dreams of a Dark Warrior is set during the events of Demon from the Dark, but from Regin and Declan’s point of view. When it was announced who Declan was in Demon from the Dark, that reveal was one of most shocking things in possibly the entire series. I wondered how in the world Kresley was going to pull off Regin and Aidan’s HEA. She has definitely accomplished that in Dark Warrior with many happy results. Even though this isn’t as steamy as her past books, don’t worry, there’s more than an abundance of passion, but more of an emphasis on the action and the incredible and witty dialogue between the characters I cannot get enough of. Again Kresley gives us great insight on why her characters act the way they do. Regin is not the spoiled brat I had though her to be, and Declan is not evil, just misinformed and unbelievably full of suffering and guilt.<br /><br />There are many familiar faces, most importantly the capture of Lothaire, the most ancient of all vampires who’s as remote and amoral as they come. Kresley has a major twist regarding him based on who his mate may be. I really thought I knew who he’d be mated with. How wrong I was! His book is next, and let me tell you, if Kresley hooks him up with whom I’m thinking she has planned, mainly based on the interactions between him and a specific character, it’s going to be the craziest and most spectacular book in this entire series! And I have no doubt that Kresley can pull it off. I wish I could tell you who I think Lothaire will be with, but that’s a humdinger of a spoiler right there. All I can say it is full of crazy awesome sauce, and this will be confusing for those who haven’t read Dark Warrior, but I do believe the black king will capture the white queen.<br /><br />It’s pretty much a given I’ll read anything Kresley Cole writes. Dreams of a Dark Warrior is another book full of win by her. *Bows down at the altar of Kresley Cole*. I’m already dying for the next book (or at least a blurb to finally know who Lothaire’s heroine is). Kudos to Kresley for another top notch book that has made me invoke my favorite phrase- “I want to have babies with it.” <br /><br />I think I want to have Kresley's babies as well.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15052260992574159364" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1605386068" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1605386068?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/26263700-dreams-of-a-dark-warrior">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dangerous-hero-themed-books-read">dangerous-hero-themed-books-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1605386068" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer691489844040632601">Whew! This was a tough one. I've struggled with how I feel about this book in the 'Immortals After Dark' series. On the one hand, it was nice to have a book that didn't follow the same recipe as the others. On the other hand, why the hell didn't it?!? I definitely had a love/hate relationship with this book. It brought out some feelings that I wasn't prepared for, to say the least.<br/><br/>Regin the Radiant meets her mate, Aidan the Fierce, when she is still a young girl. He immediately recognizes her as</span>
  <span id="freeText691489844040632601" style="display:none">Whew! This was a tough one. I've struggled with how I feel about this book in the 'Immortals After Dark' series. On the one hand, it was nice to have a book that didn't follow the same recipe as the others. On the other hand, why the hell didn't it?!? I definitely had a love/hate relationship with this book. It brought out some feelings that I wasn't prepared for, to say the least.<br /><br />Regin the Radiant meets her mate, Aidan the Fierce, when she is still a young girl. He immediately recognizes her as his mate, but recognizes that he must wait years to have her as his bride because of her youth. As she matures, he is off winning battles in order to earn his immortality. <br /><br />Eventually, she leaves the home of his parents, where he'd left her for safekeeping. She refuses to be kept by her human mate. Aidan refocuses his energy in order to find his runaway bride. He is consumed with finding her.<br /><br />When Regin grows into a lady, she seeks out her mate to satisfy her sexual cravings. Reunited with Aidan at last, the two fall easily into love. However, as Aidan has not yet earned his immortality, he cannot fully claim his bride, a daughter of gods, lest he anger them.<br /><br />Succumbing to their desires, the couple seal their fates. Aidan dies, destined to be reincarnated over and over with no memory of his former lives, or his mate. Regin is doomed to spend lifetimes searching for her male, only to lose him again every time they reconnect.<br /><br />Aidan's most recent identity is that of Declan Chase, an "officer" with The Order, a militant group looking to exterminate the immortals of the Lore. Declan is a cruel, cold-hearted, SOB. He spends his days capturing and torturing immortals in order to exact revenge for the death of his family, years earlier, at the hands of vampires.<br /><br />When Declan captures Regin, he tries fighting their connection. Yet, even he cannot deny that there is more to their attraction than meets the eye. Theirs was a case of forbidden attraction, followed by the bitterness of betrayal.<br /><br />Unlike earlier books in the series, 'Dreams of a Dark Warrior' contains some scenes of extreme abuse experienced by the heroine, largely caused by the hero. Given the history of this series, it seemed unnatural to have a male that could be so cruel to his fated mate. It also made it very hard for me to connect with Declan.<br /><br />Whereas I loved Aidan, I despised Declan. I couldn't get past the things that Declan did, no matter how much I wanted to. While he did feel remorseful at last, it was just too little too late for me.<br /><br />However, as conflicted as I felt about Aidan/Declan, I loved Regin and the supporting characters. Without a doubt, they made up for everything that Declan was lacking. I'm looking forward to hearing their stories later on in this series.<br /><br />Overall, it was still a 4-star read for me. I cannot get enough of this incredible series! On to the next one!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="691489844040632601" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2821373990157483655"><br/><br/>I really enjoy this series, but I just couldn’t for the likes of me get it to this book. So, yet again I am the odd ball in the bunch of 4 and 5 star reviews with my sad 3 stars and that’s being generous. I’m not going to get it to the story, I’m just going to tell what I did and didn’t like about the book.<br/><br/>What I didn’t like:<br/>I felt the story dragged way too much. Then just when the story was about over things were way to rushed.<br/><br/>I am so tired of books that parallels with older books in a series. </span>
  <span id="freeText2821373990157483655" style="display:none"><br /><br />I really enjoy this series, but I just couldn’t for the likes of me get it to this book. So, yet again I am the odd ball in the bunch of 4 and 5 star reviews with my sad 3 stars and that’s being generous. I’m not going to get it to the story, I’m just going to tell what I did and didn’t like about the book.<br /><br />What I didn’t like:<br />I felt the story dragged way too much. Then just when the story was about over things were way to rushed.<br /><br />I am so tired of books that parallels with older books in a series. It seems like all the bigger author now are doing this and I am tired of it. <br /><br />The torture was outrageous! I can see some of way Regin had to go through it. I either missed it, but I never caught why Chase had to go through his torture. Still I just didn’t care for Reign as a Valkrie going through all of this just for her mate. I guess I would have rather her fight for her mate another way. <br /><br />So my overall problem is. I don’t like to read my romance where the hero is betting the crap out of the heroine (even though he doesn’t know her), along with all the other violence she went though. So needless to say, I didn’t find this book one bit romantic.<br /><br />I have always enjoyed the humor Ragin had and I missed it in this book. I was hoping to have a good fun read with her and her hero.<br /><br />What I liked about this book<br />Natalya the dark fey, she was really interesting and I hope to read about her more.<br /><br />I liked reading more on Lothaire, he is really growing one me, I can’t wait for his story.<br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer151015234" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer190829660027590341"><br/><b>Excellent!! Deserves more than 5 stars!</b> <br/><br/>Loved Declan Chase, but I guess I’m a sucker for a tortured soul. Unlike the other IAD books, this one was not about finding the mate, bride, etc, because Declan and Regin’s destiny has already been established. What the book did give us was more of an insight into the Lore, and the creatures that inhabit this world. I love that some Ms. Cole’s books take place simultaneously, being that we already know the outcome of some of the characters that are mentio</span>
  <span id="freeText190829660027590341" style="display:none"><br /><b>Excellent!! Deserves more than 5 stars!</b> <br /><br />Loved Declan Chase, but I guess I’m a sucker for a tortured soul. Unlike the other IAD books, this one was not about finding the mate, bride, etc, because Declan and Regin’s destiny has already been established. What the book did give us was more of an insight into the Lore, and the creatures that inhabit this world. I love that some Ms. Cole’s books take place simultaneously, being that we already know the outcome of some of the characters that are mentioned. She is setting us up for what I believe to be a sizzling conclusion to the series, sad as it may be.<br /><br />Boy, did I laugh!! Since when is Lothaire the ‘Dr. Phil’ of the Lorean world? For someone so dreaded and evil he was somehow…compassionate?! The introduction of Thad was a pleasant surprise, and his innocence about his unknown heritage added for some humorous moments. When he was giving his ‘girl advice’ to ‘DC’, Lothaire, and Brandr, using his high school experiences…I almost fell off the chair in hysterics. I imagined the four of them hanging in bar, playing pool and swapping stories about babes. That Nix…what a hoot. She had some of her best moments in this book.<br /><br />I can’t wait to see what Ms. Cole has in store for us next.<br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer113897123" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer895985001284064284">For Indonesian crowd, read my review here : <a href='http://renslittlecorner.blogspot.com/2012/01/review-dreams-of-dark-warrior-oleh.html<br%20/>' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <b>Ren's Little Corner</b>
</a><br/><br/><b>More than 5 stars and Top Read 2012</b><br/><br/>Some big questions for me : <br/>Why it take me so long to read this?<br/>Maybe because I wait for Lothaire?<br/>Maybe its just not held my interest last year, since I'm too picky?<br/>Maybe I just tired of paranormal romance genre so I try another?<br/>Maybe, maybe, maybe...<br/><br/>Right now I just can said : I'm so ASHAMED to not read this a long time ago, when this book coming out, because Kresley Cole is gooooooood!! <b>edited</b></span>
  <span id="freeText895985001284064284" style="display:none">For Indonesian crowd, read my review here : <a href="http://renslittlecorner.blogspot.com/2012/01/review-dreams-of-dark-warrior-oleh.html&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Ren's Little Corner</b>
</a><br><br><b>More than 5 stars and Top Read 2012</b><br><br>Some big questions for me : <br>Why it take me so long to read this?<br>Maybe because I wait for Lothaire?<br>Maybe its just not held my interest last year, since I'm too picky?<br>Maybe I just tired of paranormal romance genre so I try another?<br>Maybe, maybe, maybe...<br><br>Right now I just can said : I'm so ASHAMED to not read this a long time ago, when this book coming out, because Kresley Cole is gooooooood!! <b>edited:GREAT </b>. One of my author goddes, KC show her class, again and again. I find myself to not frantic about her. Some her books like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14383.No_Rest_for_the_Wicked__Immortals_After_Dark___2_" title="No Rest for the Wicked (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">No Rest for the Wicked</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1611656.Dark_Needs_at_Night_s_Edge__Immortals_After_Dark___4_" title="Dark Needs at Night's Edge (Immortals After Dark, #4) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Needs at Night's Edge</a> (with sexy Nathan Kamp's cover) and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7098304.Demon_from_the_Dark__Immortals_After_Dark___9_" title="Demon from the Dark (Immortals After Dark, #9) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Demon from the Dark</a> are my favorite, then I realize all that books are about vampires. Kresley sure make a good and sexy vampire, not that sparkle thing if you know what I mean [wink]. Others I find it okay or yeah, or good, and I think I'm not Lykae and Demon fans. Weird, eh? At last you that love Woede's brothers and all those Highland Lykaes are save from my harem-searching-all-day-long :P.<br>That's why I don't have any expectation for this one.<br><br>Guess I'm WRONG. Because the reincarnation theme in this book is well-written. Aidan The Fierce is reborn again and again just to chase his eternally lovers, Reginleit the Radiant. But the curse always overshadow them, if Aidan's reincarnation remember his past, soon after he bedding Regin, he will die. And for his 4th reincarnation as Declan Chase (heh, a suitable name, isn't it?) fate can be cruel. Once a lover, now enemy. Since Declan is a Magister of The Order who orchestrated the Loreans capture, including Regin. But, Regin who recognize him as her lover, lure him to free her and another creatures. Even her heart want Declan, more than she want her perfect Viking. This scarful and tortured Irishman might be capture her heart as well and Regin know its Declan who she want, not Aidan.<br><br>The prologue of Dreams of a Dark Warrior tell us about how Aidan and Regin meet. How we know, even Aidan own Regin's body and soul, her heart still her own. That's why she can't love Aidan fully, while she do the otherwise with Declan. I'm glad how Miss Cole done with Declan's fate. To make him not swallowed by Aidan soul, not like the other reincarnation, so he can be himself again and finally accept what he long denied, an immortal beserker.<br><br>One thing surprised me, how I found myself to be atrracted to Lothaire! No, I never fans of Lothaire, esp when he break Lucia's neck at <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6337006.Pleasure_of_a_Dark_Prince__Immortals_After_Dark___8_" title="Pleasure of a Dark Prince (Immortals After Dark, #8) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Pleasure of a Dark Prince</a>! He seems so egois, cunning, evil, with his own agenda. But he mesmerized me with his can't-be-predicted mind. Like who he will assist at the battle. If they not take a side with him, he will fight them. I wonder who is his EndGame? And what he means with "The White Queen will never take The Black King" to Nix (who Lothaire called Phenix). So who the white queen , if The black King is Lothaire himself? We also get a hint how Lothaire always thinking about his bride. After I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10790516.Lothaire__Immortals_After_Dark___11_" title="Lothaire (Immortals After Dark, #11) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Lothaire</a> book's exceprt, I wonder if he had discovered his Bride's whereabout. And how with La Dorada? Is she truly dead or just vanished?<br><br>So many question. [sigh] After all, Dreams of a Dark Warrior is a great read that KC fans will cherish. Readers will love Regin's dry (or not) joke, Declan's tortured attitude (but after the half part, he become man who make woman swoon, sure when he not denied his original nature any longer. His "drug addict" condition might be make some readers feel uncomfortable, but I found that's its not a big deal. There just a few scenes) and other characters as well. Natalya the dark Fey, Brandr, immortal beserker, a friend of Aidan and Regin's protector and Thaddeus or Thad, an anomaly at Lore, which I assumed will be a hero for KC's YA series. Don't forget about Lothaire. Oh, and I'm so want Nix will get her own story, since we know she not mean to be with Lothaire! (I'm right, eh? [snicker])<br><br>Now the waiting for Lothaire's book which called <b>LOTHAIRE</b>, will be a torture. <b>With capital T.</b><br><br>Favorite scene :<br><br><b>Nix's message to Declan :</b><br><br><i>Begin transcript—<br><br>Testing. Hello, hellooo, anybody out there? Check, check, one, two. Soft pee. Puh, puh. Resonance! Sooooooft pee. Alpha bravo disco tango duck.<br><br>This is Nïx! I’m the Ever-Knowing One, a goddess incandescent, incomparable, and irresistible. But enough about what you think of me. It’s a beautiful day in New Orleans. The wind is out of the east at a steady five knots and clouds look like rabbits … But enough about what you think of me!<br><br>Now, down to business—<br><br>Squirrel!<br><br>Where was I? [Long pause] Why am I in Regin’s car? Bertil, you crawl right back out of that bong this minute!<br><br>Oh, I remember! I am hereby laying down this track for Magister Declan Chase. If you are a mortal of the recorder peon class, know that Dekko and I go waaaaay back, and he’ll go berserk (snicker snicker) if he doesn’t receive this transmittal. …<br><br>Chase, riddle me this: what’s beautiful but monstrous, long of tooth but sharp of tooth and soft of mind, and can never ever tell a lie?<br>That’s right. The Enemy of Old can be very useful to you. So use him already.<br><br>P.S. Your middle name’s about to be spelled r-e-g-r-e-t.<br>And with that, I must bid you adieu. Don’t worry, we’ll catch up very soon. …<br><br>[Muffled] Who’s mummy’s wittle echolocator? That’s right—you are! </i><br><br><b>Declan to Regin :</b><br><br><i>"Nothing will stop me from claiming you this night. Nothing!"<br><br>"Then you're going to widow me again? Don't you care about me?"<br><br>He gripped her nape."I fuckin' love you, Regin!" Rain spiked his lashes as he gazed down at her, commanding her, "Love me back!"<br><br>Can't lose him."J-Just wait, Aidan!"<br><br>Hies eyes went wild again; he threw back his head and roared, his neck straining.<br><br>"Please, Aidan, be calm!"<br><br>When he faced her again, he bellowed, "I'am 'no goddamned Aidan! You're talking to <b>Declan</b>. Do you no <b>see me</b>, woman?" </i><br><br>My pic of Declan : <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380337783i/695182._SX540_.jpg" width="320" height="240" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think Tom Hardy will portrayed Declan Chase perfectly ;)</span>
  <a data-text-id="895985001284064284" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('opUeAI9+YGTT8Kaiq1+Sl9ei8A5XLOtcurkij/Jis/LxrWCvJQbxbZnf5eEYIdF0Jh1J/JyJJaJBQ0QartJ8jA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  <span id="freeText7523625089379870495" style="display:none">Kresley Cole is the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of the electrifying Immortals After Dark paranormal series, the young adult Arcana Chronicles series, the erotic Gamemakers series, and five award-winning historical romances.<br /><br />A master’s grad and former athlete, she has traveled over much of the world and draws from those experiences to create her memorable characters and settings. <br />Her IAD books have been translated into 23 foreign languages, garnered three RITA awards, a RWA Hall of Fame induction, and consistently appear on the bestseller lists, in the U.S. and abroad.<br /><br />Cole lives in Florida with her family. Learn more about Kresley at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.kresleycole.com">www.kresleycole.com</a> &amp; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.thearcanachronicles.com">www.thearcanachronicles.com</a><br /><br /></span>
